// function PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        let vm = this.vm ?? {};
        vm.thinClient = thinClient.vm;
        // let httpClient = this.httpClient;

        clearInterval(thinClient.notificationIntervalId);

        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping'
        else if (location == '/shipping') shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') history();

        function shipping () {
            vm.shipping = {
                panelMessage: '',
                loadValue: '[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]',
                notificationInterval: 1800000, //30 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 1200000, //20 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 5000, //5 seconds
                videoModal: {
                    selector: '#VideoModalId',
                    zoom: {
                        in: zoomIn,
                        out: zoomOut,
                    },
                    close: videoModalClose,
                    stream: {
                        selector: '#CameraStreamId',
                        start: videoStreamStart,
                        stop: videoStreamStop,
                        captureImage: captureImage
                    }
                },
                imageFile: {
                    selector: '#CarrierLabelImageId',
                    upload: uploadCarrierLabelFile
                },
                menu: {
                    guide: {
                        inputFile: {
                            selector: '#inputFileDownload',
                        }
                    }
                },
                load: loadShip,
                customerChange: customerChange,
                getNotification: getNotification,
                selectDownloadFile: selectDownloadFile
            }
            vm.shipping.videoModal.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.imageFile.id = vm.shipping.imageFile.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.id = vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector.substring(1);

            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.imageFile.selector, uploadCarrierLabelFile);
            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector, inputFileDownloadChange);

            vm.shipping.slic = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.profile.Name.substring(0,5) : vm.profile.Name == thinClient.adminProfileName ? "XXXXX" : null;
            vm.shipping.customers = getShipperCustomers(vm.profile.Shippers);
            var enabledCustomers = vm.shipping.customers.filter(function(c) { return c.disabled != true; });
            vm.shipping.customer = enabledCustomers.length == 1 ? vm.shipping.customers[1] : vm.shipping.customers[0];
            vm.shipping.activePanel = vm.shipping.slic == undefined || vm.clientContext.Machine.Name == undefined ? 0 : 1;

            debugger;

            vm.fieldOptions = {
                Consignee: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                },
                ReturnAddress: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                }
            };
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference18.IsDisabled = true;
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.DefaultValue = vm.shipping.slic;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = vm.shipping.slic;

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (!vm.profile.FieldOptions?.Reference?.IsHidden)
                    'form[name="referenceForm"] .panel > div'.unwrap();

                'name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="poBox.isHidden()"'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="residential.isHidden()"'.remove();


                vm.shipping.getNotification();
                thinClient.notificationIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
                    vm.shipping.getNotification();
                }, vm.shipping.notificationInterval);

                if (vm.shipping.customer.disabled)
                    vm.shipping.customer.selector.focus();
                else
                    vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
            }

            function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

            function selectDownloadFile(event) {
                this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile = event.target.innerText;
                if (this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) {
                    if (this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile.slice(-3) == this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name.slice(-3))
                        updateFile();
                } else {
                    var payload = { Action: 'downloadFile', Data: this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile };
                    var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                            var data = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));

                            let linkData = `data:${data.fileType};base64,${data.encodedFile}`;
                            let downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            downloadLink.download = data.fileName;
                            downloadLink.href = linkData;
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function updateFile() {
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var request = {
                            Key: vm.shipping.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile,
                            Value: JSON.stringify({
                                fileType: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.type,
                                fileName: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name,
                                encodedFile: this.result.split(',')[1]
                            })
                        }
                        var payload = { Action: 'updateFile', Data: request };
                        var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                        thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                            if (ret.ErrorCode !== 0)
                                vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(ret.ErrorCode + " - " + ret.ErrorMessage);
                        }).catch(function (response) {
                            vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(vm.translations.Common.ErrorConnectingWCFService + ": " + response.status + " " + response.statusText);
                        })
                        vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = null;
                        $(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector).val(null);
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();

                    }
                    if (vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) reader.readAsDataURL(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected);
                }
            }

            function inputFileDownloadChange(event) {
                if (event.target.files == undefined) return;
                vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = event.target.files[0];
                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
            }

            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

            function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }


            function videoModalClose () {
                var $videoModal = $(vm.shipping.videoModal.selector);
                if ($videoModal.is(':visible'))
                    $videoModal.find('.close').click();
            }

            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

            function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }


            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

            function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }
        }

        function history() {
            vm.history = {
                searchButton: 'button:contains("Search")',
                reportSelector: '#reports'
            };

            $(document).on('click', vm.history.searchButton, selectReportChange);
            $(document).on('change', vm.history.reportSelector, selectReportChange);

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (vm.profile.Name != vm.thinClient.adminProfileName) {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;

                    let reports = [ 'Default', 'Detailed Report', 'Void Report', 'Summary Report' ];
                    vm.reports = vm.reports.filter(function(report) {
                        report.TemplateHtml = report.TemplateHtml.replace(/<span.*glyphicon-search.*<\/span>/g, '');
                        return reports.includes(report.Name);
                    });
                }
            }

            function selectReportChange(event) {
                if (vm.report?.Name == 'Summary Report') {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;
                    vm.history.carrierAcceptTableContainer = {
                        'height': $('.panel-body').height() + 'px',
                        'overflow-y': 'auto'
                    };

                    let payload = {
                        Action: 'summaryReport',
                        Data: {
                            startDate: vm.dtstart.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            endDate: vm.dtend.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            sites: getSites()
                        }
                    };
                    let data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        debugger;
                        vm.history.carrierAcceptReport = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                    });
                } else {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = false;
                }

                function getSites() {
                    let sites = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.sites.filter(function(site) { return site.Id == vm.UserInformation.SiteId;}) : vm.sites;
                    return sites.map(function(site) { return { name: site.Name }; });
                }
            }
        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function () {
        $('body').on('change', client.shipping.fileInputPaperless, this.vm, paperlessChange);
  
         function paperlessChange(e) {
             var file = e.target.files[0]
             if (file === undefined) {
                e.data.paperless = null;
             }
             else {
                 var reader = new FileReader();
                 reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                 reader.onloadend = function () {
                     e.data.paperless = { fileName: file.name, fileData: this.result.split(',')[1] }
                 }
             }                
         }       
     }

    this.BatchManager = function () {

        function clickUploadFile() {
            $('body').delegate('button:contains("Upload File")', 'click', function () {
                if ($('#fileInputField').val() != '') {
                    showSpinner();
                    var interval = setInterval(function () {
                        var msg = $('div[role="alert"]:visible');
                        if (msg.length > 0) {
                            clearInterval(interval);
                            hideSpinner();
                        }
                    }, 50);
                }
            })
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(loaded) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (loaded) {
		//debugger;
		if (loaded === '/shipping') {
			// after page sections load, set values
			$(document).ready(function() {
		        $('form[name="shippingForm"]').find('label:contains("Load")').text("Order Number");
		    });

			var generalInterval = setInterval(function () {
				// wait for general pane to load
				var generalControl = $('form[name="generalForm"]');

				if (generalControl.length > 0) {
					clearInterval(generalInterval);
					generalControl.append('<div class="col-md-6">' +
					'<div class="no-left-right-padding form-group" style="left:-1px;"property="custom_markup" model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19" caption="Markup Percentage">' +
					'<label class="markup-padding">Markup Percentage</label>' + 
					'<input id ="custom_markup_id" type="text" class="form-control">' +
					'</div>' +
				  	'</div>');
				}
			}, 50);
		}

	};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// PrePrint(doc, localPort, viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PrePrint = function(doc, localPort, viewModel){
        // WORKAROUND for bug where printer profile doesn't send optional settings
    	// attach control string to set defaults to start of document string
    	if((doc.DocumentSymbol == 'UPSAPI.UPS.PACKAGE_LABEL.STANDARD') && doc.RawData){
        	var printerDefaults = "^XA^LH0,0^XSY,Y^MD30^XZ\n";
        	var oldraw = atou(doc.RawData[0]);
        	var newraw = printerDefaults + oldraw;
        	doc.RawData[0] = utoa(newraw);
    	}
    };

            client.shipping.consignee.searchAddresses.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.SearchAddresses);
            client.shipping.consignee.validateAddress.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.ValidateAddress);

        }
    }

// function appendCSS() // returns undefined
function appendCSS(){
        var style = document.createElement('style');
        style.innerHTML = 'input:focus, textarea:focus, select:focus{background-color: #ffffcc;}';
        style.innerHTML += 'li.active a.ng-binding { background-color: #dddddd !important; }';
        document.head.appendChild(style);
    }

// function dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined
function dismissAlertDialog() {
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) {
            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// function client.init() // returns undefined
init: function () {          
            String.prototype.addButtonLabel = function(text) {
                var interval = setInterval(function(selector) { 
                    var $element = $(selector);
                    if ($element.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);                        
                        $element.parent().removeClass('col-md-3');
                        $element.parent().addClass('col-md-4'); 
                        $element.wrap('<label class="ng-binding">').after(text);
                    } 
                }, 10, this);
            }
        }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {

    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $(function()
      {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val('DOCUMENTS');
        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CheckForThirdPartyBilling();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

// ShowContainerTable(tableIndex) // returns undefined
      ShowContainerTable: function (tableIndex)
      {
        try
        {
          var currentContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible');
          var targetContainer;

          /* fallbackContainer is used when the last table in the container is reached.  Go back to the beginning on 'next', to the end on 'prev'. */
          //var fallbackContainer;
          var uiNavButton;

          //console.log($('span.current-container-index.container-val').text());
          var currentContainerIndex = parseInt($('span.current-container-index.container-val').text());

          switch (tableIndex)
          {
            case 'prev':
              // targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + ($(currentContainer).index() - 1) + ')');
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + (currentContainerIndex - 2) + ')');


              //fallbackContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').last();
              uiNavButton = $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').first();
              break;

            case 'next':
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + ($(currentContainer).index() + 1) + ')');
              //fallbackContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').first();
              uiNavButton = $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.nextPackage();"]').first();
              break;

            default:
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + tableIndex + ')');
              break;
          }

          // if (targetContainer.length === 0) {
          //   targetContainer = fallbackContainer;
          // }

          $(uiNavButton).click();

          $(currentContainer).fadeOut(200).hide().promise().done(function ()
          {
            var rows = $(targetContainer).find('tr').length;
            if (rows > 2)
            {
              $(targetContainer).find('tr.empty-table').hide();
            }
            $(targetContainer).fadeIn(200).show().promise().done(function () { UpdateItemCounts(); });
          });

          /* Update the text to show 'Container X of Y'.  .index() + 1 as the index is 0 based. */
          $('span.current-container-index').text($(targetContainer).index() + 1);

          /* Now get the box associated with the table and change the select option. */
          var selIndex = $(targetContainer).data().SelectedIndex;

          $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex', selIndex);

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
        }
      }

// GetWeightFromScale(callback) // returns undefined
function GetWeightFromScale(callback)
  {
    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function()
    {
      /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
      if ($.isFunction(callback)) callback;
    });
  }

// InitElements() // returns undefined
InitElements: function()
      {
        /* Create the Consolidate Orders button dynamically. */
        /* This is done on the post load for my customer as they want to have a primary order loaded first. */
        /* With each consolidated order being added, I am comparing the consignee to the primary order to confirm this order is going to the correct consignee. */
        $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left').append($('<button />')
          .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
          .attr('id', 'buttonConsolidateOrders')
          .text('Consolidate Orders').fadeIn());

        /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
        $('body').delegate('#buttonConsolidateOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        });

        /* Customer uses a scanner that appends the <enter> key after the scan.  This delegate fires when that happens. */
        $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function(e)
        {
          var keycode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which;
          if ((keycode == 13) | (keycode == 9))
          {
            ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
          }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseConsolidatedOrdersWithoutSaving', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
        });

      }

// ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog() // returns undefined
ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog: function()
      {
        Tools.ShowOverlay();

        /* Get rid of any existing options. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').empty();

        /* Add whatever orders are already in the Shipper Reference to the select box. */
        var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
        var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        $(arrayOrders).each(function(a, b)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders')
            .append($('<option />')
              .val(b)
              .text(b)
              .removeClass('not-processed')
              .addClass('processed')
              .css('color', '#265ca1'));
        });

        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function()
        {
          /* Clear the input box, then focus on it. */
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
        });

      }

// CloseDialogWithoutSaving() // returns undefined
CloseDialogWithoutSaving: function()
      {
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').empty();
        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();
        /* HideLoader will hide the loader as well as the overlay. */
        Tools.HideLoader();
      }

// PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds) // returns Promise<number>
PollDomForElement: async function(element, timeoutInSeconds = 10)
      {
        var t = parseInt(timeoutInSeconds * 5);
        var i = 0;

        return new Promise((resolve, reject) =>
        {
          var checkExist = setInterval(function()
          {
            i++;

            if ($(element).length > 0)
            {
              /* Stop the timer. */
              clearInterval(checkExist);
              resolve(1);
            }

            /* The loop has timed out. */
            if (i == t)
            {
              clearInterval(checkExist);
              reject(new Error('Operation timed out waiting for ' + element + ' to attach to the DOM.'));
            }

          }, 200);

        });
      }

// SetCurrentViewModel(viewModel, callback) // returns undefined
SetCurrentViewModel: function(viewModel, callback)
      {
        user = new User(viewModel.UserInformation, true);
        currentViewModel = viewModel;
        if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }
      }

// WaitForElement(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
WaitForElement: async function(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await Tools.PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function(promiseResult)
        {
          if (defaultValue) { $(element).val(defaultValue); }

          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (waitThenFocus == true) { $(element).focus(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          console.log('WaitForElement()', error);

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// FocusOnLoadInput() // returns undefined
FocusOnLoadInput: function()
      {
        Tools.WaitForElement('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]', true, null, null);
      }

// ShowOverlay() // returns undefined
ShowOverlay: function()
      {
        if ($('div.overlay').length === 0)
        {
          //console.log('div.overlay not found, creating');
          $('div.body-content').first().append($('<div />').addClass('overlay').css(
            {
              content: '',
              position: 'fixed',
              top: 0,
              left: 0,
              width: '100vw',
              height: '100vh',
              'background-color': 'rgba(0, 0, 0, .25)',
              'z-index': 1049
            })).show();
          /*
          .overlay {
            content: '';
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100%;
            height: 100%;
            background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, .25);
            z-index: 1049;
          }
        */
        }
        else
        {
          $('div.overlay').show();
        }
      }

// HideOverlay() // returns undefined
HideOverlay: function()
      {
        $('div.overlay').hide();
      }

// ShowErrorAlert(ErrorMessage) // returns undefined
ShowErrorAlert: function(ErrorMessage)
      {
        var divAlert = $('<div />').attr('id', this.GetRandomAlphaNumericString());

        $(divAlert).addClass('alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom alert-danger ng-scope')
          .css(
            {
              'z-index': 1550,
              cursor: 'pointer'
            })
          .attr('role', 'alert')
          .append($('<button />').attr('type', 'button').addClass('close')
            .append($('<span />')
              .attr('aria-hidden', 'false').text('x'))
            .append($('<span />').addClass('sr-only').text('Close')))
          .append($('<div />')
            .append($('<div />').addClass('ng-scope alert-message').text(ErrorMessage)
              .prepend($('<span />').css('padding-right', '10px').addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert custom-error-icon'))));

        $('body').append($(divAlert).show());
        /*
          <button type="button" class="close" onclick="$(this).closest('div').hide();">
            <span aria-hidden="false">×</span>
            <span class="sr-only">Close</span>
          </button>
          <div>
            <div class="ng-scope alert-message"></div>
          </div>
        */
      }

// GetRandomAlphaNumericString() // returns string
GetRandomAlphaNumericString: function()
      {
        /* When using this function to create unique element id's.  Keep in mind that id's can't start with a number, I prefix 'se' here for that reason. */
        return 'se' + (+new Date()).toString(16).slice(-12);
      }

// GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, stringDelimiter) // returns Array<string>
GetUniqueArrayFromString: function(inString, stringDelimiter = ',')
      {
        var trimArray = $.grep(inString.split(stringDelimiter), function(a)
        {
          return a.trim().length > 0;
        });

        /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
        trimArray = trimArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
        return trimArray;
      }

// GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray(inArray) // returns string
GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray: function(inArray)
      {
        /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
        var uniqueArray = inArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
        var newUniqueString = '';

        $(uniqueArray).each(function(a, b)
        {
          if (b.trim().length > 0)
          {
            newUniqueString += b.trim() + ',';
          }
        });

        return newUniqueString;
      }

// GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(inString) // returns string
GetUniqueCSVStringFromString: function(inString)
      {
        var uniqueArray = this.GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, undefined);
        return this.GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray(uniqueArray);
      }

// Sleep(ms) // returns Promise<void>
Sleep: function(ms)
      {
        return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
      }

// ParseEncodedData(data) // returns Promise<any>
ParseEncodedData: async function(data)
      {
        let deferred = $.Deferred();

        //nothing came back from the server.
        if (!data) deferred.resolve('No data passed to parser');

        let parseResult = $.parseHTML(data.Data || data)[0].textContent;

        //best guess that the return was json.  parse as json and return
        let f = parseResult.slice(0, 1), l = parseResult.slice(-1);
        let bJsonFirst = ((f.indexOf('{') !== -1) || (f.indexOf('[') !== -1));
        let bJsonLast = ((l.indexOf('}') !== -1) || (l.indexOf(']') !== -1));

        if (bJsonFirst && bJsonLast) { deferred.resolve($.parseJSON(parseResult)) }

        //if the result of the parse was a number, return an integer (may need to change this to a float (++ instead of +)
        //note:  don't parse as float unless you know it's a float.
        //do this in the dev tools console:
        //let pf = '7'; console.log('pf as int', +(pf)); console.log('pf as float', ++(pf));
        //else, return the string
        deferred.resolve($.isNumeric(parseResult) ? +(parseResult) : (parseResult));

        return deferred.promise();
      }

// MakeUserMethodRequest(MethodName, MethodData, callback) // returns Promise<any>
MakeUserMethodRequest: async function(MethodName, MethodData, callback)
      {
        let defjam = $.Deferred();

        let m = {};
        m.ServerMethod = MethodName;
        m.MethodData = MethodData || null;

        let u = this.GetUserObject();

        var ajaxObject = {
          UserContext: u.UserContext || await u.GetUserContext(),
          Data: JSON.stringify(m)
        };

        $.ajax(
          {
            url: u.UserMethodUrl,
            method: 'POST',
            dataType: 'json',
            data: ajaxObject,
            headers: u.GetRequestHeaders()
          }).done(function(data)
          {
            let t = Tools.ParseEncodedData(data).then(function(result)
            {
              defjam.resolve(result);
            });

          }).fail(function(xhr)
          {
            defjam.reject('Error in ajax call');
            console.log(xhr);
            console.log('Method name: ', MethodName);
            console.log('Method data: ', MethodData);
          });

        return defjam.promise();
      }

// InitElements(LogToServer) // returns undefined
      InitElements: function (LogToServer)
      {
        /* Create the Consolidate Orders button dynamically. */
        /* This is done on the post load for my customer as they want to have a primary order loaded first. */
        /* With each consolidated order being added, I am comparing the consignee to the primary order to confirm this order is going to the correct consignee. */
        $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left')
          .append($('<button />')
            .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
            .attr('id', 'buttonConsolidateOrders')
            .text('Consolidate Orders')
            .fadeIn());

        /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
        $('body').delegate('#buttonConsolidateOrders', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function (e) 
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        });

        /* Customer uses a scanner that appends the <enter> key after the scan.  This delegate fires when that happens. */
        $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function (e)
        {
          var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
          if (keycode == 13 | keycode == 9) 
          {
            ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
          }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseConsolidatedOrdersWithoutSaving', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
        });        


        /* Logging to the server only works with SBR, set to false if not using SBR's with a custom logging method. */
        Tools.SetServerDebugMode(LogToServer);
      }

// ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog() // returns undefined
      ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog: function ()
      {
        Tools.ShowOverlay();

        /* Get rid of any existing options. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').empty();

        /* Add whatever orders are already in the Shipper Reference to the select box. */
        var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
        var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        $(arrayOrders).each(function (a, b)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(b)
            .text(b)
            .removeClass('not-processed')
            .addClass('processed')
            .css('color', '#265ca1'));
        });

        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function () 
        {
          /* Clear the input box, then focus on it. */
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
        });
      }

// AddOrderNumbersToList() // returns undefined
      /* This takes the order number from the input box and adds it to the select box. */
      AddOrderNumbersToList: function ()
      {
        var inVal = $('#textOrderNumber').val();
        var bExists;

        /* Do not add duplicate entries to the select box. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function ()
        {
          if (this.text == inVal) 
          {
            bExists = true;
            /* Break out of the .each loop. */
            return false;
          }
        });

        if (bExists == true)
        {
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
          return false;
        }

        /* The order number is unique, add it to the select box. */
        if (inVal.length > 0)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(inVal)
            .text(inVal)
            .addClass('not-processed')
            .trigger('change'))
            .promise().done(function ()
            {
              $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
            });
        }
      }

// SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers() // returns undefined
      SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          var ordersToQuery = '';

          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders > option.not-processed').each(function ()
          {
            ordersToQuery += $(this).text() + ',';
          });

          /* Done creating the list of orders to get from the server which is now held in the ordersToQuery variable. */

          /* Hide the div. */
          $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

          /* Make sure there are orders in the list. */
          if (ordersToQuery.length > 0)
          {
            //ConsolidatedOrders.GetOrderInformationFromCustomer(ordersToQuery);
            Tools.MakeUserMethodRequest('GetOrderInformation', ordersToQuery, true, this.ProcessDataFromCustomer);
          }
          else
          {
            Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: No unique orders to pull from the server.  All consolidated orders have already been added to this shipment.');
          }

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// ProcessDataFromCustomer(jsonData) // returns undefined
      ProcessDataFromCustomer: function (jsonData)
      {
        try
        {
          $(jsonData).each(function (a, b)
          {
            /* For testing, this is set to '!== true' so it will return order data.  This needs to be set to '=== true' for any other case. */
            if (ConsolidatedOrders.CheckForMatchingConsignee(b) == true)
            {
              var currentPackage = Tools.GetCurrentPackage();
              if (!currentPackage)
              {
                Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR:  Could not add commodities to package for order ' + b.orderId + '.  See error console for details.');
                return false;
              }
              ConsolidatedOrders.UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(b.orderId, b.orderNumber);
            }
            else
            {
              Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR 500:  Could not add commodities for order ' + b.orderId + '.  Address mismatch.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
          console.log(error);
        }
      }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderId, OrderNumber) // returns undefined
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderId, OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var inputConsigneeReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderId;
        var consigneeReferenceVal = $(inputConsigneeReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        
        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
        var newConsigneeReferenceString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(consigneeReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputConsigneeReference).val(newConsigneeReferenceString);
      }

        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

        Tools.HideLoader();
      }

      }

// WaitForElement(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns undefined
      WaitForElement: async function (element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if (defaultValue) { $(element).val(defaultValue); }

          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (waitThenFocus == true) { $(element).focus(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForElement()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForSelectOptions(selectElement, optionLength, indexOptionToSelect, stringOptionToSelect, bClearFirst, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns undefined
      WaitForSelectOptions: async function (selectElement, optionLength = 1, indexOptionToSelect, stringOptionToSelect, bClearFirst, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {

        if (indexOptionToSelect && stringOptionToSelect)
        {
          throw new error('Cannot use both indexOptionToSelect and stringOptionToSelect.  Please use only one option and try again.');
        }

        if (bClearFirst) { $(selectElement).val([]); }

        var element = selectElement + ' option:gt(' + optionLength + ')';

        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (indexOptionToSelect) { $(selectElement + ' option').eq(indexOptionToSelect).prop({ 'selected': 'selected' }); }

          if (stringOptionToSelect) { $(selectElement).val(stringOptionToSelect); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForSelectOptions()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForTableRows(table, tableRowsNeeded, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns undefined
      WaitForTableRows: async function (table, tableRowsNeeded = 1, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        var element = table + ' tr:gt(' + tableRowsNeeded + ':visible)';

        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForTableRows()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForInputValues(inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns undefined
      WaitForInputValues: async function (inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await PollInputsForValues(inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForInputValues()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        console.log(vm);
        GetUserContext();
        if(location === '/shipping'){
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $terms = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]');
                var loaded = $terms.length;
                if (loaded) {
                    //removeDropDown();
                    
                    $('body').delegate('#AddMultiplePackages', 'click', function () {
                        AddMultiplePackagesModel();
                    });
                    
                     $('body').delegate('#MultiCloseModal', 'click', function () {
                        MultiCloseModal();
                    });
                    
                    $('body').delegate('#AddMultiPackagesReal', 'click', function () {
                        AddMultiPackagesReal();
                    });
                    
                    clearInterval(interval);
                }
            }, 50);
            
        }
    }

//START

/*get user context data */
function GetUserContext(userContext) {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
    return userContext;
}

function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

//segregate user data by userid(so by default, users will only see their own account)
function userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria)
{
    var userContext;
    userContext = GetUserContext(userContext);
    searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 0 });
}

//Shipexec function
this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
    userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria);
};


//END
    
}

    };

    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        appendCSS();
        debugger;
        getUserContext();
        dismissAlertDialog();
        pageLoaded = true;
        debugger;
        if (location == "/shipping") {
            tpbTransportationChargesAddressBookEntries = getAddressBookEntries('Third Party Billing', this.vm.UserInformation);
            vm.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressBookEntries = tpbTransportationChargesAddressBookEntries;

            vm.changeTransportationCharges = this.ChangeTransportationCharges;


            // $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] input[name="PostalCode"]', 'keydown', function() {
            //    alert('hello');
            //});

            // Domestic Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges1"]', 'change', function () {
                var vm = this.vm;
                debugger;
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]');
                //  alert($billOption.val());
                //  console.log("Value: " + $billOption.val());


                if ($billOption.val() == "thirdParty") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    //$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                } else {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                }
            });

            var tpbSelectedIndex = 0;
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress1"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {
                console.log("HERE44545");

                setTimeout(function () {

                    console.log("Index: " + tpbSelectedIndex);
                    var tpbSelect = document.querySelectorAll('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]');
                    tpbSelect[0].selectedIndex = tpbSelectedIndex

                }, 1500);


            });

            // International Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes1"]', 'change', function () {
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]');
                //   alert($billOption.val());
                if ($billOption.val() == "thirdParty") {

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                } else {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress1"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {
                $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });

            var startTime = new Date();
            var pageLoaded = setInterval(function () {
                if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                    clearInterval(pageLoaded);
                    //    console.log('clearinterval');
                } else {
                    var tpbFound = false;
                    var consigneeFound = false;
                    var $thirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');
                    var $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');

                    if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.length && tpbSearchAddress.length) {
                        tpbFound = true;
                    }

                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;


                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0) {
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                            //International
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
