                    }
                }
            }, 125);
        }
    };

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();


    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        //shipperReferenceKeyUp();
        miscReference7KeyUp();
        replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(this.vm.profile.BoxTypes);

        $('body').delegate(client.shipping.addPackageButton, 'keyup', function (e) {

            if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                //client.shipping.shipperReference.focus();
                client.shipping.miscRef7.focus();
            }
        })


        function shipperReferenceKeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.shipperReference, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }

        function miscReference7KeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.miscRef7, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }


        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }




    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();
	
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

		//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
        //this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
	
        //this.vm.overrideOptimization = pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6)
        pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6);
	
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		checkAndSetShipDateTest(this.vm);
		
        this.vm.arriveByDate = client.shipping.arriveByDate;
        client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();

        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
			
			console
            return date;
        }
		
		function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.overrideOptimization = false;
        this.vm.arriveByDate = '';
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

		

        //check and set the CPD checkbox here
        checkAndSetCPD(this.vm);


        //check for CPD flag here, set checked if true
        function checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) {
            //create interval here to watch for CPD checkbox
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $cpdCB = $('[ng-model="vm.cpdProcessFlow"]');

                if ($cpdCB.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var cpdFlag = sessionStorage.getItem("cpdflag");
                    //status can be True, False or Null

                    if (cpdFlag == "true") {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = false;
                    }


                }
            }, 10)

        }

		
    }

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        this.vm.getWeight();

        if (this.vm.cpdProcessFlow) {
            //$(client.shipping.shipperReference).focus().select();
            $(client.shipping.miscRef7).focus().select();
        }
        else {
            client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
        }
    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {

        //Set the CPD flag to whatever state the this.vm.CPDWorkflow state is
        sessionStorage.setItem("cpdflag", this.vm.cpdProcessFlow);
    }

// GetUserName() // returns the matched email string array or null
    function GetUserName() {
        var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
        return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i);
    }

        this.getUserContext();

        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }


            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }


            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },
            replaceText2: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerText = this.innerText.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },
             replaceLabel2(selector, oldText, newText) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('label') === oldText) {
                        $(this).attr('label', newText);
                    }
                });
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {

// function translateDates() // returns undefined
        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

// function getCurrentMonthYear(action) // returns null
            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }

// function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns string
            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

// function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns string
            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

         function deliverDatePicker() {

            translateToFrench = {

                  "September": "Septembre",
                  "October": "Octobre",
                  "November": "Novembre",
                  "December": "Décembre"
                },
                "Days": {
                  "Sunday": "Dimanche",
                  "Monday": "Lundi",
                  "Tuesday": "Mardi",
                  "Wednesday": "Mercredi",
                  "Thursday": "Jeudi",
                  "Friday": "Vendredi",
                  "Saturday": "Samedi"
                }
              };

            var datePicker = $('div.uib-daypicker');

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(translateToFrench['Months'])) {

                    currentMonth.text(currentMonth.text().replace(key, value));
                }
            }



            datePicker.find('th small').each(function () {
                $(this).text(translateToFrench.Days[this.innerHTML]);
            })
        }

// function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() // returns undefined
    function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() {
        // Check if the flag is already true, which means we no longer need to change the selects
        if(canadaSelected || !isSelectedValueInShippersArray()) {
          return; // Exit the function if Canada has been selected in all dropdowns or if the site is not from Canada
        }
        
        // Get all select elements with the name 'Country'
        var selects = document.querySelectorAll('select[name="Country"]');
        var allSelected = true; // To keep track if all selects have been set to Canada
      
        // Iterate through the NodeList
        selects.forEach(function(select) {
          // Only set the value to 'string:CA' if it's not already set
          if (select.value !== 'string:CA') {
            select.value = 'string:CA';
            allSelected = false; // Not all selects have been set to Canada
      
            // Trigger change event for AngularJS
            if ('createEvent' in document) {
              var evt = document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');
              evt.initEvent('change', false, true);
              select.dispatchEvent(evt);
            } else {
              select.fireEvent('onchange');
            }
          }
        });
      
        // If all selects have been set to Canada, set the flag to true
        if (allSelected) {
          canadaSelected = true;
        }
      }

// function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() // returns boolean
      function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() {
        // Use a more specific selector that targets the ng-model
        var selectElement = document.querySelector('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]');
        
        // Ensure the element exists
        if (!selectElement) {
          console.warn('Select element not found');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the index of the selected option
        var selectedIndex = selectElement.selectedIndex;
        
        // Ensure an option is selected
        if (selectedIndex < 0) {
          console.warn('No option is selected');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the selected option element
        var selectedOption = selectElement.options[selectedIndex];
        
        // Get the value of the selected option (and remove the "string:" prefix if present)
        var selectedValue = selectedOption.value.replace('string:', '');
        
        // Check if the selected value is in the array
        return StoreLocationsCanadaArray.includes(selectedValue);
      }

// function GetUserName() // returns array|null
function GetUserName() {
   var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
   return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i);
}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {   
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); })
        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"], button[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"]', translateDates);
        $('a[href="/Manage"][title="Manage"]').remove();

        
        setInterval(function() {
            translateDates();
            $('button').each(function() {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let text = $(this).text().trim();
                let month = text.split(' ')[0];

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-info.uib-datepicker-current.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Today') {
                        $(this).text('Aujourd\'hui');  // Translate "Today" to French
                    }
                });
                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-danger.uib-clear.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Clear') {
                        $(this).text('Effacer');  // Translate "Clear" to French
                    }
                });

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-success.pull-right.uib-close.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Close') {
                        $(this).text('Fermer');  // Translate "Close" to French
                    }
                });
                
        
                for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                    if (month.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                        $(this).prop('disabled', true);  // Disable the button if it contains a month name
                        return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 1500);

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
            client.init(); 
            clearInterval(intervalId);
        }, 1000);

        switch(location) {
            case '/shipping':
                this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = "Créer un envoi";
                break;
            case '/history':
                $("h4:first").text("Historique");
                
                break;
            // Add more cases as needed
        }
     }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') this.History();
        else if (location == '/closemanifest') this.CloseManifest();
        else if (location == '/manifestdocuments') this.ManifestDocuments();
        else if (location == '/transmit') this.Transmit();
        else if (location == '/groupmanager') this.GroupManager();
        else if (location == '/managedata') this.ManageData();
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function () {
        translateSelectAddressBookOption();
        this.vm.pickupRequestButtonCaption = client.translateToFrench['Pickup Request'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = client.translateToFrench['Create a Shipment'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Reset = client.translateToFrench['Reset'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Continue = client.translateToFrench['Continue'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Clear = client.translateToFrench['Clear'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.SelectAction = client.translateToFrench['Select Action'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Add = client.translateToFrench['Add'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Update = client.translateToFrench['Update'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Today = 'hello'

        function translateSelectAddressBookOption () {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $selectAddressBook = $('form[name="addressForm"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"] option[label="Select address book"]');
                if ($selectAddressBook.length >= 3) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $selectAddressBook.each(function () {
                        if (client.translateToFrench[this.text] !== undefined) {
                            $(this).attr('label', client.translateToFrench[this.text]);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    }

// History() // returns void
this.History = function () {

            $('#reports option').each(function () {
                if (client.translateToFrench[this.text] !== undefined) {
                    $(this).attr('label', client.translateToFrench[this.text]);
                }
            });
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest)
  {

    var tableHeaderRowCount = 1;
    var table = document.getElementById('miTabla');
    console.log("table size: ")
    if (table && table.rows)
    {
      var rowCount = table.rows.length;
    } else
    {
      var rowCount = 0
    }

    for (var i = tableHeaderRowCount; i < rowCount; i++)
    {
      table.deleteRow(tableHeaderRowCount);
    }

  }

    this.NewShipment();

// PostSearchHistory(packages) // returns void
this.PostSearchHistory = function(packages) {
    var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
        {
          if ($('table[ng-table="vm.tableParamsForDetailed"] tr').length > 1)
          {
            clearInterval(checkExist);
            $('table[ng-table="vm.tableParamsForDetailed"] tr:gt(1)').find('td:eq(2) > div:not(.ng-hide)').html(function() 
            {
                var trackingN = $(this).text().trim();
                
                
              if(trackingN.startsWith('1Z')) {
              return "<a href=https://wwwapps.ups.com/WebTracking/track?track=yes&trackNums=" + $(this).text().trim() + "&requester=ST/trackdetails target='_new'>" + $(this).text().trim() + "</a>";
              }   else {
              return "<a href=https://online.chrobinson.com/tracking/#/?trackingNumber=" + $(this).text().trim() + "&requester=ST/trackdetails target='_new'>" + $(this).text().trim() + "</a>";
              }
            });
          }
        }, 100);
    }

// NextPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.NextPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {  
    $('select[name="SubClassNumbers'+eval(packageIndex-1)+'"]').empty();
    $('select[name="NMFCNumbers'+eval(packageIndex-1)+'"]').val('');  

    shipmentRequest.Packages[eval(packageIndex-1)].MiscReference19 = ''; 

    }

// PreviousPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.PreviousPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {		  
    $('select[name="SubClassNumbers'+eval(packageIndex+1)+'"]').empty();   
    $('select[name="NMFCNumbers'+eval(packageIndex+1)+'"]').val(''); 
    shipmentRequest.Packages[eval(packageIndex+1)].MiscReference19 = '';
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (callUserMethod(1) == 'supervisor') {
            this.vm.fieldOptions["MiscReference3"].IsDisabled = false;
        }
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference12 = userEmail;

        // general visibility
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].NotificationFailureAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // ship notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // delivery notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // delivery exeption notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // return delivery notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        if (location == '/') {
            var w = window.location.href + "batchmanager";
            window.location.replace(w);
        }

        if (location == '/batchmanager') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $.globalEval('var userContext;');

                var dataObject = {};
                dataObject.Action = "GetDealerId";
                dataObject.Content = "";
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (jsonData) {
                    debugger;
                    //console.log(jsonData.Data);
                    $('body').find('a[ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').first().trigger('click').promise().done(function (e) {
                        ProcessDealerId(jsonData.Data);
                    });
                });
            }); //end document.ready
        }

        if (location == '/batchdetail') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                try {
                    $('body').delegate('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.')
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var tdDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (tdDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                } //end if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) 

                            } //end if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) 

                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () 
                        //   { 
                        //     ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   });
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');


                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }

    } //end PageLoaded

// BatchManager() // returns undefined
this.BatchManager = function() {
        debugger;

        // set user email
        var userEmail = $("div.navbar-collapse").text();
        userEmail = userEmail.match(/([a-zA-Z0-9._-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+\.[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+)/gi).toString();
        $("#email").val(userEmail);
        $("#email").change();

        IPSUploadFile();

        function IPSUploadFile() {
            $('body').delegate('#ipsUploadFile', 'click', function () {
                alertMessage('info', "Rate Process Started, an email will be sent upon completion");
                showSpinner();
                var vm = $(this).attr('vm')
                if (ensureLoadIPS(vm)) {
                    var fileName = cbr.loadIPS.file.name.split('.')[0];
                    debugger;
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.readAsDataURL(cbr.loadIPS.file);
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var data = {
                            'UserContext': cbr.userContext,
                            'Data' : JSON.stringify({
                                'Action': 'Rate',
                                'Shipper': cbr.loadIPS.shipper,
                                'ShipDate': cbr.loadIPS.shipDate,
                                'Email': cbr.loadIPS.email,
                                'FileName': fileName,
                                'EncodedFile': this.result.split(',')[1],
                            })
                        }

                        $.post({ 
                            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                            data,
                            headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                        }).done(function (result) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            if (result.ErrorCode > 0) {
                                alertMessage('danger', response.ErrorMessage);
                            } else {
                                alertMessage('success', "Rate Completed");
                                loadIPSReset();
                            }
                        }).fail(function (err) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            alertMessage('danger',"The process is taking longer than usual to complete but will continue to run on the server until the rate file is complete");
                        });	
                    }
                }
                // hide the spinner after 15 seconds
                setTimeout(function(){
                    hideSpinner();
                }, 15000);
            });
        }

        function loadIPSReset() {
            $.each( cbr.loadIPS, function(name, value){
                $('[ng-model="vm.loadIPS.' + name + '"]').val(null);
            });
        }

        function ensureLoadIPS(vm) {
            var msg = [];
            var result = true;

            if (vm == '') {
                msg.push('Please update all options and try again.');
            } else {
                cbr.loadIPS = JSON.parse(vm);
                //if (cbr.loadIPS.type == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Select Rate or Address Validation radio button.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipper == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Missing Shipper.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipDate == undefined) msg.push("\u2022Missing Ship Date.");
                if (cbr.loadIPS.email == undefined) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing Email Address.');
                } else {
                    if (invalidEmailAddress(cbr.loadIPS.email)) msg.push('\u2022Email Address is invalid.')
                }

                var files = $('#ipsFileInputField').prop('files');
                if (files.length == 0) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing File.')
                } else {
                    cbr.loadIPS.file = files[0];
                }
            }

            if (msg.length > 0) {
                result = false;
                alertMessage('danger', msg.join("<br />"));
                hideSpinner();
            }
            
            return result;
        }
    }

// ManifestDocuments() // returns void
    this.ManifestDocuments = function () {
        testbutton();

        function testbutton() {
            $('body').delegate('#buttonExportCODFile', 'click', function () {
                debugger;
                var shipper = $(this).attr('shipper');
                var carrier = $(this).attr('carrier');
                var historyId = $(this).attr('historyId');
                var historyShipDateYear = $(this).attr('shipDateYear');
                var historyShipDateMonth = $(this).attr('shipDateMonth');
                var historyShipDateDay = $(this).attr('shipDateDay');
                var isSftpChecked = $('#SftprBtnId').prop('checked');
                var isLocalChecked = $('#LocalrBtnId').prop('checked');
                debugger;

                // Send data to user method on the server side
                var usermethodParams = { "action": 1, "usercontext": client.userContext, "shipper": shipper, "historyId": historyId, "historyShipDateYear": historyShipDateYear, "historyShipDateMonth": historyShipDateMonth, "historyShipDateDay": historyShipDateDay, "carrier": carrier, "sftpSelectrdStatus": isSftpChecked, "localSelectrdStatus": isLocalChecked };
                var codFileString;

                var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
                
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
                    debugger;                  

                    //****New code 01.24.2022****
                    var jsonString = $("<textarea/>").html(response.Data).text();

                    if (jsonString && isLocalChecked) {                        
                        codFileString = jsonString;

                        var data = new Blob([codFileString], { type: 'text/plain' });

                        var ie = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE\s([\d.]+)/),
                            ie11 = navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7.0/) && navigator.userAgent.match(/rv:11/),
                            ieEdge = navigator.userAgent.match(/Edge/g),
                            ieVer = (ie ? ie[1] : (ie11 ? 11 : (ieEdge ? 12 : -1)));

                        // set the export file name 
                        var exportFileName = "ShipmentRequest" + historyShipDateYear + historyShipDateMonth + historyShipDateDay + "_1_" + shipper + ".txt"

                        if (ieVer > -1) {
                            window.navigator.msSaveBlob(codFileString, exportFileName);

                        } else {
                            var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.download = exportFileName;
                            downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(data);
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(link);
                        }
                    }
                });          
            })
        }
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

// this.ShowLoadModal() // returns void
this.ShowLoadModal = function()
  {
    $("#load-modal-bg").show();
    $("#load-modal").show();
  }

// this.HideLoadModal() // returns void
this.HideLoadModal = function()
  {
    $("#load-modal-bg").hide();
    $("#load-modal").hide();
  }

// this.ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
ShowAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    let that = this;
    //get rid of any previous entries
    $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

    //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
    //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

    //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
    this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;

    //get all the commodities in the shipment from all packages
    this.goods = $(this.packages).map(function(x, y)
    {
      return y.CommodityContents;
    });

    //loop the goods array and update the markup within the slideout panel
    $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
    {
      //debugger;
      let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      b.GoodsKey = k;

      if (b.packageIndex === undefined) {
        // initial index is undefined after loading order, default to fix NaN bug later
        b.packageIndex = 0;
      }
      //copy the source element
      let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).attr({ 'hash-key': b.$$hashKey, 'goods-key': b.GoodsKey, 'pkg-index': b.packageIndex }).removeAttr('id');

      //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
      //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
      let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

      $(item).find('.goods-description').text(b.Description);
      $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>' + b.Quantity + '</strong>');
      $(item).find('.goods-unit-of-measure').text(b.QuantityUnitMeasure + ', ');
      $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + cost + '</strong> ' + b.UnitValue.Currency + ')');
      $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(+(b.packageIndex) + 1);
      $(item).find('.header-logo').show();

      //append it to our list
      $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

      //show it gracefully
      $(item).show();

    });

    //create a working array object so we can manipulate the data non-destructively
    this.working = $.makeArray(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.goods)));

    $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
    $('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();
  }

// this.HideAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
HideAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    // restore the shipping panel sizes first, doing this last sometimes caused a scope issue and left pane wasn't getting resized
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6');
    let u = $('#divAssignCommodities').outerWidth() + 100;
    //$('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('destroy');
    $('#divAssignCommodities').animate({ left: -u }, 400, function() { $(this).hide(); });
  }

// this.ApplyCommodityAssignments() // returns void
ApplyCommodityAssignments()
  {
    let that = this;

    //every list item will have a pkg-index attr, get that highest value to determine how many pkgs we need
    //don't use pkg-status.length because that will include multiple commodities and the end result will be wrong
    let packed = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[pkg-status=packed]');

    //first get all the pkg-index attributes, then get the highest number and add one
    let pkgs = $(packed).map(function(x, value) { return +$(this).attr('pkg-index') }).toArray();
    let pkgCount = Math.max(...pkgs) + 1;

    while (this.packages.length < pkgCount)
    {
      //the vm.addPackage isn't firing, just click the button
      $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function(e) { });
    }

    //loop the pkg count, get the commodities for that pkg, write the objects to the vm CommodityContents object
    for (let p = 0; p < pkgCount; p++)
    {
      let w = $.grep(this.working, function(item, i) { return item.packageIndex == p });
      this.packages[p].CommodityContents = w;
    }

    //click the General tab
    $('li[heading=General]:visible a').first().click();
    this.HideAssignGoodsPane();

    //after we are done, move back to the first package in the shipment
    while ($('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text() !== '1')
    {
      $('button[ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').first().click();
    }

  }

// this.GetClassViewModel() // returns the view model object
GetClassViewModel()
  {
    //the goods data is going to come from vm.currentShipment.Packages[pkgIndex].CommodityContents as an array
    return this.viewModel
  }

// this.CancelSplitOfPackages(li) // returns void
CancelSplitOfPackages(li)
  {
    //hide the split modal and clear the input value
    $('.escape-target').hide();
    $(li).find('.split-pkgs-modal').hide().find('input[type=number]').val([]).focus();
    $(li).find('.btn-show-split-form, .assign-to-pkg').fadeIn();
  }

// this.InitiateDelegates() // returns void
InitiateDelegates()
  {
    let that = this

    $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
    });

    $('body').delegate('.btn-show-split-form', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let div = $(this).closest('div').find('.split-pkgs-modal').first();
      $(div).tooltip({ container: 'body' });

      $(div).css('display', 'flex').fadeIn();
      $('.split-pkgs-modal:visible').find('input').first().focus();

      //hide the split button now...and the input
      $(this).hide();
      $(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('input.btn-go-split-pkgs', 'click', function(e)
    {
      console.log('btn-go-split-pkgs click event handler');

      let li = $(this).closest('li').first();
      let div = $(this).closest('div').first();

      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text('1');

      //val - 1 as the first entry will be the first package
      let v = $(div).find('input[type=number]').first().val();

      that.UpdateGoodsObject(v, li);

      $('.split-pkgs-modal').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
    });

    //if the user escapes out of the split modal, hide the modal and show the previous forms
    $('body').delegate('.split-pkgs-modal', 'keydown', function(e)
    {
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 27)
      {
        //need to show the previous input and button now
        let li = $(this).closest('li');

        that.CancelSplitOfPackages(li);
      }
    });

    //if the user presses enter or tab in the num-of-items number input, move to the next one
    //these are the number inputs after the items have been split across packages
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-items-in-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-items-in-pkg keydown focusout event handler');

      $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 13 || keycode === 9)
      {
        //disable the input, update the commodity object, focus on the next box input
        //$(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').focus();
        that.UpdateListItemPackageQuantities($(this).closest('li'));
      }
    });

    //user hits enter in the input box, click the button for them
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-pkgs-to-use', 'keyup keydown', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-pkgs-to-use keyup keydown event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');

      $(btn).attr('disabled', $(this).val() < 2);

      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        //let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');
        $(btn).trigger('click');
      }
    });

    //this was formerly .scan-input.  as of 9/24/2022, removing the split functionality completely
    //with this change, only need to get the numerical value out of the input
    $('body').delegate('.assign-to-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.assign-to-pkg keydown focusout event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      debugger;
      if (keycode == 13 || keycode == 9 || e.type == "focusout") //enter
      {
        e.preventDefault();
        //pull only the number from whatever was passed.  make sure it is greater than 0 since we can't assign a good a pkg zero.
        const val = $(this).val().replace(/[^1-9]/g, '');

        let li = $(this).closest('li');
        
        if (val)
        {
          //console.log('assigning this to ', val);
          //assign the integer to the line item header (not shown, but may be shown in the future)
          //this one is easy, just assign the pkg-index attr to whatever they scanned.  when the apply button is clicked it will assign the commodities
          //let li = $(this).closest('li');
          $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text(val);
          $(li).find('button').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
          $(li).attr('pkg-index', val - 1);
          $(li).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

          //find the matching item in the this.working array and update the package index
          let item = $.grep(that.working, function(good, i) { return good.$$hashKey == $(li).attr('hash-key') })[0];
          item.packageIndex = val - 1;
          //return;
        }
        // set focus to next li input box
        if (e.type !== "focusout") {
          $(li).next().find('.assign-to-pkg').focus().change();
        }
      }
    });

    $('#btnAssignCommodities').on('click', function(e)
    {
      if ($('#divAssignCommodities').is(':visible')) return;
      that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
    });
  }

// GetUserContext() // returns void
function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
}

// ajaxGet(url) // returns result
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen/Ambient Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

              position: fixed;
              top: 0;

            }
          */
                } else {
                    $('div.overlay').show();
                }
            }

// this.Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(1, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
            
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();
        
        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

        //Adding commodities automatically.
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CommodityContents = [];
                            
                            var newCommodity = {
                                Description: "UN3373 Biological Substance,Cat B",
                                Quantity: 1,
                                QuantityUnitMeasure: "EA",
                                UnitWeight:
                                    {
                                        Amount: 0.5,       
                                        Units: "KG"         
                                      },
                                UnitValue:{
                                    Amount:5,
                                    Currency:"GBP"
                                } , 
                                OriginCountry: "GB",
                                RestrictedArticleType:32,
                                HarmonizedCode:"3002901000",
                                ProductCode:"UN3733"
                            };
                                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CommodityContents.push(newCommodity);
                                setTimeout(function(){
                                                $('[value="Save"]').trigger('click');
                                },200);

    }

this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
