// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen/Ambient Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) {
                client.$divReference3.hide();
                client.$divReference3.find('input').val('');
                client.vm.currentShipment.Packages[client.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3='';
            }
            else {
                client.$divReference3.show();
            }
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        this.clearSessionState();
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
        that.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();
        debugger;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 = "28454 Livingston Ave";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City ="VALENCIA";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince ="CA";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company ="Dock 1 Specimen Processing";

       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact = "Q2 Solutions";

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country = "US";

       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode = "91355";
        
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone  = "9194052248";
         
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
         
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// LoadStudyReferenceCodeDialog() // returns void
LoadStudyReferenceCodeDialog: function () {

                Tools.ShowOverlay();

                /* Get rid of any existing options. */
                $('#selectShipper').empty();

                $('#divModalLoadShipments').fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function () {
                    $('#selectShipper').focus();
                });
            }

// CloseDialogWithoutSaving() // returns void
CloseDialogWithoutSaving: function () {

                $('#divModalLoadShipments').hide();

                Tools.HideLoader();
            }

// FocusOnLoadInput() // returns void
FocusOnLoadInput: function () {
                var loadInput;
                if ($('#inputLoadValue').length > 0) {
                    loadInput = '#inputLoadValue';
                } else {
                    loadInput = 'input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]';
                }
                this.WaitForElement(loadInput, undefined, undefined, true);
            }

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];

                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];

                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Marken_Phase2_CBR_2500.cs
// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        //Declaring variables.
        var custom1_values, custom1, custom2, custom3, custom4, custom5, custom6, customData;
        var customValues = {};
        var customKeysArray = [];
        var CustomData_AfterCustom4 = [];
        var item;

        customData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        // Iterate over the CustomData array and map values to their respective keys
        $.each(customData, function (index, item) {
            customValues[item.Key] = item.Value;
        });

        if (this.vm.profile.Name == 'Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile') {
            for (var i in customData.length) {
                item = customData[i];
                customKeysArray.push(item.Key);
            }

            var startIndex = -1;
            // Find the index of the key "Custom5"
            for (var i = 0; i < customData.length; i++) {
                if (customData[i].Key === "Custom5") {
                    startIndex = i;
                    break;
                }
            }

            // If "Custom5" is found, start storing values from it onwards
            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                for (var j = startIndex; j < customData.length; j++) {
                    CustomData_AfterCustom4.push(customData[j].Value);
                }
            }

            // Now, customValues object contains all custom values accessible by their keys
            var custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            var custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
            var custom3 = customValues['Custom3'];
            var custom4 = customValues['Custom4'];
            var custom5 = customValues['Custom5'];
            var custom6 = customValues['Custom6'];
        } else {
            //debugger;
            custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
        }

        //Checking DryIceRequired sets true via User Custom1 data.
        if (custom1.split(',').length > 1) {
            custom1_values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom1, ',');
        } else {
            throw new Error("Custom1 is not Comma delimited string.");
        }

        //Setting the Leg1Shipper
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = custom1_values[0];

        //Creating Dry Ice Required Checkbox
        if ($('#DryIceRequired').length == 0 && custom1_values[1] == "true") {
            //Adding DryIceRequired checkbox and its label.
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<input />', {
                type: 'checkbox',
                id: 'DryIceRequired',
                name: 'DryIceRequired'
            }));
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<label />', {
                for: 'DryIceRequired',
                text: 'Dry Ice Required'
            }));
        }

        //Comparing the User Custom2 with the Profile enabled Services and remove the unmatched services from the Service UI.
        var arrayValues_custom2;
        if (custom2 != null || custom2 != undefined) {
            arrayValues_custom2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom2, ',');
            var matchedValues = [];
            var profileServices = this.vm.profile.Services;
            profileServices.forEach(function (value1) {
                var serviceExists = arrayValues_custom2.some(function (value) {
                    return value1.Name.indexOf(value) !== -1;
                });
                if (serviceExists) {
                    matchedValues.push(value1);
                }
            });

            //Populating the Matched services on the Service UI.
            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mySelect = $('select[multiple="multiple"][property="Service"]');
                mySelect.empty(); //Clearing the existing Services listed out in the Service UI list.

                for (var i in matchedValues) {
                    mySelect.append($('<option></option>').attr('value', matchedValues[i].Symbol).text(matchedValues[i].Name));

                }
            });
        }

        //Retrieving Custom Data values after CustomData4(Leg2 Companies).
        var CustomDataCount = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length;

        var CustomData_FirstValues = []; //Fetch the First strings from Customdata after Custom4.
        var CustomData_OtherValues = []; //Fetch the rest of other strings from Customdata after Custom4.

        // Loop through each inner array in CustomData_AfterCustom4
        for (var i = 0; i < CustomData_AfterCustom4.length; i++) {

            var customData = CustomData_AfterCustom4[i];

            //var customData_values = customData.Value;

            var valuesArray = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(customData, ',');

            var firstValue = valuesArray.shift().trim();

            //Store the first string from the Custom data.
            CustomData_FirstValues.push(firstValue);

            //Store the remaining values
            CustomData_OtherValues.push(valuesArray.map(val => val.trim()));
        }


        //debugger;
        //Enabling the MiscReference1 field based on Profile.
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {

           // debugger;

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";
                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').hide();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').hide();
                }
                else {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').show();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').show();
                }

            });

            //Creating Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox
            if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').length == 0 && custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                    $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                        'type': 'checkbox',
                        'id': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn',
                        'name': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn'
                    }),
                    $('<label />').attr('for', 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').text('Central Labs Frozen Samples Return')
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);

            }
            else {
                //Creating Empty Packaging Checkbox
                if ($('#EmptyPackaging').length == 0) {
                    //debugger;
                    var checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                        $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                            'type': 'checkbox',
                            'id': 'EmptyPackaging',
                            'name': 'EmptyPackaging'
                        }),
                        $('<label />').attr('for', 'EmptyPackaging').text('Empty Packaging')
                    );

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty);

                }



                //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Empty Packaging Checkbox is checked.
                $('body').delegate('#EmptyPackaging', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#EmptyPackaging').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "true";
                    } else {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "false";
                    }
                });
            }


            //Setting Leg2 Dry Ice weight hidden by default
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
            });
            //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox is checked.
            $('body').delegate('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn', 'change', function (e) {
                if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').is(':checked')) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "true";

                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').show();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').show();

                } else {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "false";
                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
                }
            });

            //Creating Leg2 Dry Ice Weight
            if ($('#Leg2DryIceWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:120px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Dry Ice Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:140px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }

            //Setting MiscReference10 to true if Leg2 Dry Ice Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2DryIceWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10 = $(this).val();
            });
            //Creating Leg2 Package Weight
            if ($('#Leg2PackageWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:70px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Package Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:90px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }
            //debugger;
            //Setting MiscReference9 to true if Leg2 Package Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            $('#divModalCompanyPopup').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            //Manual Upload
            var commodityLists = GetCommodityContents();
            $.each(commodityLists.CommodityContents, function (index, option) {
                var textMessage = commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].Description + ' ' + commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].HarmonizedCode;

                $('#commodityKey').append($('<option>', {
                    value: JSON.stringify(option),
                    text: textMessage
                }));
            });

            $('#addButton').one('click', function () {

                var showMessage = $('<div>').attr('id', 'displayMessage').text("Commodity added").css('font-weight', 'bold');
                $('.manualUpload').after(showMessage);

                var quantity = $('#quantity').val();
                if (quantity % 1 !== 0) {
                    alert("Qty is invalid");
                }
                else {
                    //Store Quantity in MiscReference15
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference15 = quantity;
                }

                //Store commodity content in Misc Reference14
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#commodityKey').val();
            });

            //Creating Service Dropdown if User Custom4 is present.
            var hasCustom4 = false;
            for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length; i++) {
                if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[i].Key === "Custom4") {
                    hasCustom4 = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (hasCustom4) {
                if (custom4 != '' && custom4 != 'undefined' && custom4 != null && $('#Service').length === 0) {
                    //Creating Service Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect1 = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Service').text('Service: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Service',
                            'name': 'Service'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect1);

                    var arrayOfValues_custom4 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom4, ',');

                    if (arrayOfValues_custom4.length > 1) {
                        $.each(arrayOfValues_custom4, function (i, e) {
                            $('#Service').append($('<option>', {
                                value: e,
                                text: e
                            }));
                        });

                        $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                            'class': 'spacer'
                        }));

                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Custom4 is not comma-delimited.");
                    }
                }
            } else {
                alert("Custom4 is not present");
            }


            //Use case: 5 User Custom data fields -> Leg2 companies will be present only at the custom5 field.
            var CustomData5_FirstValues = [];
            var CustomData5_OtherValues = [];

            //if (CustomDataCount == 5) {
            //debugger;
            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                var custom5_Values = [];
                custom5_Values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom5, ',');
                var custom5_firstValue = custom5_Values.shift().trim();

                //Store the first value
                CustomData5_FirstValues.push(custom5_firstValue);

                // Store the remaining values
                CustomData5_OtherValues.push(custom5_Values.map(val => val.trim()));
                //debugger;
                $('#CompanyName').val(custom5_Values[0]);
                $('#CompanyContact').val(custom5_Values[1]);
                $('#CompanyAddress').val(custom5_Values[2]);
                $('#CompanyCity').val(custom5_Values[3]);
                if (custom5_Values.Length > 7) {
                    //debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[6]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[7]);

                } else {
                    // debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val("");
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[6]);

                }

                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    //debugger;
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";
                        CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                            //debugger;
                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CustomData5_OtherValues.toString();

                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                        });
                    }
                });
            }


            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                if ((custom5 != '' && custom5 != 'undefined' && custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' && custom6 != 'undefined' && custom6 != null)) {
                    //Creating Company Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Company').text('Company: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Company',
                            'name': 'Company'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    //$('div.modal-body').prepend(labelAndSelect);
                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect);



                    $.each(CustomData_FirstValues, function (i, e) {
                        $('#Company').append($('<option>', {
                            value: e,
                            text: e
                        }));
                    });

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                        'class': 'spacer' // Ensure you define this class in your CSS with the desired spacing
                    }));

                    // Event listener for company selection change
                    $('body').delegate('#Company', 'change', function (e) {
                        //debugger;
                        var selectedCompany = $(this).find(":selected").val();
                        CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);
                    });

                    // Trigger change event on company dropdown to populate corresponding values by default
                    $('#Company').trigger('change');

                }

                //If Leg2LabelRequired check box is checked, setting MiscReference6 to true and populating the Company and Service values on the Modal.
                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";

                        if ((custom4 != '' || custom4 != 'undefined' || custom4 != null) || (custom5 != '' || custom5 != 'undefined' || custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' || custom6 != 'undefined' || custom6 != null)) {

                            CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                                var com = CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);

                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = com.toString();
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                            });
                            $("#buttonCompanyPopup").click();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            //debugger;
            //Setting Leg1 and Leg2 PDF Invoice default by False.         
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";


        } else {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";

                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            //Setting Leg1 PDF Invoice default by False
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

        }
        //debugger;
        //Assigning the User address to Return Address
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
        //this.vm.profile.Shippers= this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        //Assigning the Weight Units to "KG" if Ship From country is not US.
        //debugger;
        var selectedShipper = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper; //$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
        var map = $.grep(this.vm.profile.Shippers, function (shipper) {
            console.log(shipper.Symbol);
            return shipper.Symbol == selectedShipper;
        })[0];
        if (map.Country != "US") {
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Units = "KG";
        }
        
        
         //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    
                     var total=0;
                for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                    total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                }
                var inst=[];
                inst.push(total);
                debugger;
				shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions=inst[0].toString();
               
                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });
        
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns no value
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        $(document).on('click', '[ng-click="vm.ok()"]', function(){
       debugger;
       
           var total=0;
           var quan=0;
           var unitValue=0;
           var com= shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents;
           for(var item=0; item<com.length; item++){
               quan=com[item].Quantity;
               unitValue=com[item].UnitValue.Amount;
               total += parseFloat(quan)* parseFloat(unitValue);
           }
         
           $("#totalComm").text(total);
        });
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns no value
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.clearSessionState();
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
        that.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        
        StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
        $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
        
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        else if (location == '/shipping') {

            Tools.HideLoader();
            this.Shipping();
        }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {
            
            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if(e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box') 
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
         }
 
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;
        
        
            $(document).ready(function() {
               
             $("#OK").on("click", function() {
            
                 var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if(arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)){
                     var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue); 
                     var selectedStudy= arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                     //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                     
                     var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                     var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                      shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                      
                     var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                     var selectedSite= arrayOrders2[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                }
                else
                 {
                     alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                     throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                 }
        
                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                 GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);
                
                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                
            });
        
        });
     
    }

// Source: MarkenLLP2 (MLLP2)_Inbound Returns CBR_EU_TO_UK_1916.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        
        StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
        $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
        
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        else if (location == '/shipping') {
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
            this.Shipping();

            $('[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]').trigger('click');
            setTimeout(() => {
                $('[ng-click="vm.ok()"]').trigger('click');
            }, 100);
            
            //Creating new paragraph element for adding the label at the bottom.
            var newParagraph = $('<p>', {

                id: 'appendText',

                style: 'font-weight:bold',

                text: 'Pickup Latest Time Ready cannot exceed: '

            });
            $('div.col-md-8').append(newParagraph);
            var currentText = newParagraph.text();
            var appendedText = currentText + this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[3].Value;
            $('#appendText').text(appendedText);

        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(1, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
         }
        
        $('[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]').trigger('click');
        setTimeout(() => {
            $('[ng-click="vm.ok()"]').trigger('click');
        }, 100);

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[3].Value; //Maximum Pickup Latest Time Ready

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;
        
        
            $(document).ready(function() {
               
               $("#OK").on("click", function() {
            
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if(arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)){
                     var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue); 
                     var selectedStudy= arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                     //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                     var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                      shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                      
                     var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                     var selectedSite= arrayOrders2[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.

                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                }
                else
                 {
                     alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");

                 }

// Source: McIlHenny Revised (MCILHENNYREVISED)_McIlHenny Client Side Rules_1687.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {  
        if(window.location.hash == "#!/shipping")
        {
            var checkExist=setInterval(function()
            {
                if(window.jQuery)
                {
                    /* Stop the timer */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                     $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) { $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide(); });
                }
            },50);
        }    
    }

// Source: McKinsey & Co., Inc (mcKinsey)_McKinsey Reference Rule_64.cs
// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        
        // Change error text for ConsigneeReference
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
             {
                var consignee = $('input[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]');
                if (consignee.length) 
                {
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    consignee.siblings('.errorText').text("Charge code not authorized. For business shipping purposes only");
                }
            }, 500);
        }
        
        appendCSS();
        //getUserContext();
        dismissAlertDialog();
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function() {
    updateDryIceRegulationSet();
    function updateDryIceRegulationSet() {
        debugger;
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.hazmatdryIceBtn"]', 'click', function() {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $dryIceRegulationSet = $('[ng-model="vm.dryIceInfo.DryIceRegulationSet"]');
                if ($dryIceRegulationSet.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $dryIceRegulationSet.find('option[label="Regulations Not Specified"]').remove();
                }
            }, 50);
        });
    }
};

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) 
    {            
        //Services configured in Pending Shipments Profile Field Options
        var backup2DADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; //UPSAPI.UPS.2DA        
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpeditedIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS        

        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, 
        function(e) 
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference5).change();
            if (e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service) 
            {
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference8"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').val(backup2DADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]').val(backupNDADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]').val(backupExpeditedIntlService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val(backupExpressIntlService).change();
            }
        });
    };

// Source: Meta Platforms Facebook (METAPLATFORMSFACEBOOK)_Meta Return Client Rules Phase 2_1857.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        client.hideMenu();
        client.hideHyperlink();
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        else if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.isMobile = isMobile;
        this.vm.metaBase64 = client.meta.imageBase64;
        this.vm.confirmationMessage = 'We have received your request and will ship boxes out to you soon.  Please check your personal email for shipping confirmation.'
        this.vm.clearNameAddress = clearNameAddress;
        //update fieldoption stateprovince validationdropdown for custom list
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.StateProvince'].ValidationType = 5;
        this.vm.updateConsigneeStateProvince = updateConsigneeStateProvince;
        this.vm.focusNext = focusNext;
        this.vm.onChangeAssetType = onChangeAssetType;        
        this.vm.addReturnItem = addReturnItem;        
        this.vm.clickedPage = clickedPage;
        this.vm.buildPage = buildPage;
        this.vm.removeReturnItem = removeReturnItem;
        this.vm.returnInstructions = [
            'Please use the below drop-down menu to select the return package and input Meta Asset Tag number or Device Serial Number. For Prototype device, please select the best fit dimension package.',
            'Please only pack one item per package.'
        ]

        function isMobile () {
            var regex_mobile = new RegExp(/Android|BlackBerry|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Opera Mini|IEMobile/, 'i');
            var userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent;
            return regex_mobile.test(userAgent)
        };  

        function buildPage () {
            this.dataWithPagination = [];
            var start = (this.pagination.currentPage-1)*this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            var end = start + this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            for (var i = start; i < end; i++) {
                var item = this.dataArray[i];
                if (item != undefined) {
                    this.dataWithPagination.push(item);
                }
            }            
        }

        function clickedPage(e) {
            if (e.target.classList.contains('active')) return;
            this.pagination.currentPage = parseInt(e.target.innerText);
            this.buildPage();
        }        

        function removeReturnItem(index){
            this.dataWithPagination.splice(index, 1);

            var pageIndex = this.pagination.currentPage - 1;
            var pageDataArrayIndex = pageIndex*this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            this.dataArray.splice(pageDataArrayIndex + index, 1);

            if (this.dataWithPagination.length == 0) {
                this.pagination.currentPage = pageIndex;
            }

            this.pagination.numberOfItems = this.dataArray.length;
            this.pagination.numberOfPages = Math.ceil(this.pagination.numberOfItems/this.pagination.itemsPerPage);
            this.buildPage();            
        }

        function addReturnItem () {            
            var item = {
                AssetType: this.selectedAssetType, 
                BoxSize: this.selectedBoxSize, 
                AssetTagOrSerialNumber: this.assetTagOrSerialNumber
            }
            if (!isComplete(item)) return;
            this.dataArray.push(item);
            this.pagination.numberOfItems = this.dataArray.length;

            var pageCount = Math.ceil(this.pagination.numberOfItems/this.pagination.itemsPerPage);
            if (this.pagination.numberOfPages != pageCount) {
                this.pagination.numberOfPages = pageCount;
                this.pagination.currentPage = pageCount;
                this.dataWithPagination = [];
            }
            
            if (this.dataWithPagination.length == this.pagination.itemsPerPage) {
                this.pagination.currentPage = this.pagination.numberOfPages;
                this.buildPage(); 
            } else {
                this.dataWithPagination.push(item);
            }
            this.clearSelectedReturns();
            $('[ng-model="vm.selectedAssetType"]').focus();
        }

        function focusNext () {
            var activeNgModel = document.activeElement.attributes['ng-model'].value;
            var textArray = $('[type="text"]');
            for (var i = 0; i < textArray.length - 1; i++) {
                var ngModel = textArray[i].attributes['ng-model'].value;
                if (ngModel == activeNgModel) {                    
                    textArray[i+1].focus();
                    return;
                }
            }
            $('button[name="addReturnItem"]').focus();
        }
        
        function onChangeAssetType () {
            var selectedBoxId = this.selectedAssetType.BoxSizeId;
            var boxIndex = $.map(this.boxSize, function(box, index){
                if (box.Id == selectedBoxId) { return index;}
            });
            this.selectedBoxSize = this.boxSize[boxIndex];
         
            this.assetTagOrSerialNumber = this.selectedAssetType.Code == 'LD' ? 'N/A' : '';
            this.readonlyAssetTagOrSerialNumber = this.selectedAssetType.Code == 'LD';

            var returnItem = { AssetType: this.selectedAssetType, BoxSize: this.selectedBoxSize, AssetTagOrSerialNumber: this.assetTagOrSerialNumber };
            isComplete(returnItem);
        }

        function isComplete(item) {
            var result = false;
            if (item.AssetType == '' || item.AssetType.BoxSizeId == 999)
                $('[ng-model="vm.selectedAssetType"]').focus();
            else if (item.BoxSize == '' || item.BoxSize == undefined)
                '[ng-model="vm.selectedBoxSize"]'.focus(); //wait to focus
            else if (item.AssetTagOrSerialNumber == '') {
                $('[ng-model="vm.assetTagOrSerialNumber"]').focus();
            }                
            else 
                result = true;
            return result;
        }
        
        function updateConsigneeStateProvince(country) {
            this.consigneeStateProvince = [];
            if (country == 'US') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.unitedStates;
            else if (country == 'CA') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.canada;
            this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Phone'].IsRequired = country == 'CA';
        }

        function clearNameAddress(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
            if (nameAddress == 'Consignee') {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
                    Company: this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Company'].DefaultValue,
                    Email: client.userName
                }
                shipmentRequest.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = '';
            }
            client.shipping.contact.focus();
        }
    }

// clickedPage(e) // returns void
        function clickedPage(e) {
            if (e.target.classList.contains('active')) return;
            this.pagination.currentPage = parseInt(e.target.innerText);
            this.buildPage();
        }        

// buildPage() // returns void
        function buildPage () {
            this.dataWithPagination = [];
            var start = (this.pagination.currentPage-1)*this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            var end = start + this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            for (var i = start; i < end; i++) {
                var item = this.dataArray[i];
                if (item != undefined) {
                    this.dataWithPagination.push(item);
                }
            }            
        }

            this.dataArray.splice(pageDataArrayIndex + index, 1);

        }

// onChangeAssetType() // returns void
        function onChangeAssetType () {
            var selectedBoxId = this.selectedAssetType.BoxSizeId;
            var boxIndex = $.map(this.boxSize, function(box, index){
                if (box.Id == selectedBoxId) { return index;}
            });
            this.selectedBoxSize = this.boxSize[boxIndex];

            var returnItem = { AssetType: this.selectedAssetType, BoxSize: this.selectedBoxSize, AssetTagOrSerialNumber: this.assetTagOrSerialNumber };

        }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        client.shipping.contact.focus();
        
        this.vm.clearSelectedReturns = clearSelectedReturns;
        this.vm.pagination = {
            currentPage: 1,
            itemsPerPage: 6,
            numberOfPages: 1
        };        
        this.vm.tableheight = 40*this.vm.pagination.itemsPerPage+20;
        this.vm.dataArray = [];
        this.vm.dataWithPagination = [];
        this.vm.consigneeStateProvince = [];
        this.vm.selectedReturnItem = '';
        this.vm.returnItemQuantity = '';
        this.vm.readonlyAssetTagOrSerialNumber = false;
        this.vm.returnItems = client.meta.returnItems;
        this.vm.assetType = client.meta.assetType;
        this.vm.boxSize = client.meta.boxSize;
        this.vm.clearSelectedReturns();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Company: this.vm.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Company'].DefaultValue,
            Email: client.userName
        }
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = '';

        function clearSelectedReturns() {
            this.selectedAssetType = { BoxSizeId: 999 };
            this.selectedBoxSize = '';
            this.assetTagOrSerialNumber = '';
        }
    }

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    //debugger;
                    pageLoaded = true;
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 100);

            setFocus(loadText);
        }
    };

    };

                consigneeCompany = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');

                var $generalTab = $('general-tab');
                generalCarrierInstructions = $generalTab.find('[property="CarrierInstructions"]');
                generalDescription = $generalTab.find('[property="Description"]');
                generalDimensionLength = $generalTab.find('[name="length"]');
                generalDimensionWidth = $generalTab.find('[name="width"]');
                generalDimensionHeight = $generalTab.find('[name="height"]');

                $internationalTab = $('international-tab');
                internationalWorldEaseHeading = $internationalTab.find('h5:contains("World Ease")');


                // var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && generalCarrierInstructions.length && generalDescription.length &&
                //     generalDimensionLength.length && generalDimensionWidth.length && generalDimensionHeight.length && $accessorialsTab.length;

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && generalDescription.length && internationalWorldEaseHeading.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    pageLoaded = true;
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 100);

            setFocus(consigneeCompany);
        }
    };

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        this.vm.dimensionChange = this.DimensionChange;
        this.vm.nameAddressChange = this.NameAddressChange;

        // shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA' };

        shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = '';

        shipmentRequest.glCodeFileDownload = this.GLCodeUserMethod;

        if (pageLoaded) {
            this.vm.dimensionChange(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging);
        }

        setFocus(consigneeCompany);
    };

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {

        //uncomment this to auto get weight
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        debugger;

        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }//end of this.shipping

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');

        $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

        $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', false);
    }

// function getUserContext() // returns void
    function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
                loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');  
                
                var loaded = loadText.length;
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            
        appendCSS();

        this.vm.loadWeight = loadWeight;
        
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                };


            } else {
                client.alert.Danger(this.translations.Common.ErrorCode + " : " + ret.ErrorCode + "  " + ret.ErrorMessage);
            }            
        }
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
        this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.vm.loadWeight();
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
        {
            var loadInterval = setInterval(function()
            {
                loadText = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                if (loadText.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(loadInterval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]', 'keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13 && $(this).val().indexOf(".") !== -1)
                {
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[1]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[2]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[0]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                }
            });
        }
    };

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

                {

                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[2]).change();

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Consignee Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms == "CONSIGNEE")
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').focus();
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 == "RTGD")
        {
            alert("Please ensure to rate and select the desired service for shipping.");
        }
    };

        setFocus(loadText);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "SHIPPER";
    };
