// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location == "/shipping") {
            // Select PPO vs Non-PPO
                    
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]', 'change', function () {
                var $referenceOptions = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]');
                if ($referenceOptions.val() === "PPO") {
                    //alert("PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = true;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference14"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("NIKE Cost/Profit Center Bill To")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15"]').hide();


                    $('label:contains("C/N CARTON ID NUMBER 1 Per Carton")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').show();
                    $('label:contains("PO# (Begins with 35, 45)")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').show();
                } else if ($referenceOptions.val() === "Non-PPO") {
                    //alert("Non-PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = false;

                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("PO# (Begins with 35, 45)")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').hide();
                } else {
                    //alert("blank" + $referenceOptions.val());

                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = false;

                    $('label:contains("")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').hide();
                }
            });
            // Domestic Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]', 'change', function () {
                
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]');

                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();//.hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                    alert($billOption.val());
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();

					});

        	HighlightWrongOrderNumber();

				if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
			});
			let i = emailText.indexOf("@");
			if(emailText.substring(0, i)==='demo0')
			{ ReplaceAccountNumberWithXXXXXX();} 
        }
        
        if(globalVar === '/closemanifest'){
            // Provide a default label function to avoid "undefined" in the select
            vm.getManifestLabel = function(item) {
                // Show nothing or a placeholder until real data is loaded
                return item && item.Name ? item.Name : '';
            };

        }
        
	}

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;
        var validCostCenterExists = true;
        if (!ValidateCostCenterAccount()) {
            validCostCenterExists = false;
        }
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2 = getEmployeeId();
        this.vm.profile.Shippers = validCostCenterExists? getShippersFromCostCenter() : [];
        checkElmLoaded('form[name="visibilityForm"]').then((elm) => {
            if ($('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryMethod"]').length === 0) {
                addShipperRelease();
            }
        });
        if(!validCostCenterExists)
        {
             throw new Error("User data: Total cost centers are not matching with the shippers.");
        }

    };

// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns undefined
    ShowAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let that = this;

      //get rid of any previous entries
      $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

      //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
      //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

      //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
      this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;
      this.goods = this.json.data.map(m => m.boxes).flat();
      this.goods.sort((a, b) => { return a.skuId - b.skuId });

      //loop the commodities to create a master list item for each
      $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
        b.UniqueId = k;

        //copy the source element
        let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).data(b);

        //change the id of the main containing element so we don't run into issue later
        //each clone is a discreet list item which corresponds to a commodity
        $(item).attr('id', k);

        //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
        //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
        //let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

        $(item).find('.goods-sku').html('SKU: <strong>' + b.skuId + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('Quantity: <strong>' + b.quantity + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('Unit Cost: <strong>$' + b.unitPrice + '</strong>');

        //append it to our list
        $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

        //assign all goods to the first package
        that.packages[0].CommodityContents.push(that.GetCommodityContentObject(b));

        //update the weight and declared value in the root of the object
        let weight = that.packages[0].Weight;
        let dva = that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount;
        const thisWeight = (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs);
        const thisValue = (+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice);

        if (!weight.Amount) { weight.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].Weight.Amount += (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs).toFixed(2);

        if (!dva.Amount) { dva.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += Math.round((+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice) * 100) / 100;

        //show it gracefully
        $(item).show();
      });

      //that.UpdatePackageCounts();
      //$('li[heading=Goods] a:first').click();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
      $('.scan-input:visible').first().focus();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
    }


// HideAssignGoodsPane() // returns undefined
    HideAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let u = $('#divAssignCommodities').outerWidth() + 100;
      $('#divAssignCommodities').animate({ left: -u }, 400, function() { $(this).hide(); });
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6');
    }


// InitiateDelegates() // returns undefined
    InitiateDelegates()
    {
      let that = this

      $('body').delegate('#btnAssignCommodities', 'click', function()
      {
        if ($('#divAssignCommodities:visible').length > 0) return;
        that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-new-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done((e) =>
        {
          const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
          that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
        });
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-current-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.undo-box-assignment', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, 1);
      });

    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
		var licenseTab;
		var documentsMethodsTab;
		var DDTCTab;
		
		//HIDE LICENSE TAB
		//HIDE Documents Methods TAB
		//HIDE DDTC TAB
		if (location === '/shipping') {
			var interval = setInterval(function () {
				
				var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("li"); 
				
               Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("License")) licenseTab = tag;
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Documents Methods")) documentsMethodsTab = tag;
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("DDTC")) DDTCTab = tag;
                   });
				
				if (licenseTab && documentsMethodsTab && DDTCTab) {
				    clearInterval(interval);
				    //licenseTab.style.display = "none"; 
				    documentsMethodsTab.style.display = "none";
				    //DDTCTab.style.display = "none";
			    }
			    
			}, 50); 
		 }
    }

// Source: Powder Valley (POWDER_VALLEY)_Powder Valley Client Business Rules_1658.cs
// myMethod() // returns undefined
function myMethod() {
        if ($('#ordersPerPage').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#ordersPerPage').val("10");
        }
        if ($('#pageNumber').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#pageNumber').val("1");
        }
        if ($('#dateAfter').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#dateAfter').val("2021-01-01");
        }
        if ($('#batchType').val().trim() === "" || $('#batchType').val().search("undefined") > -1) {
            $('#batchType').val("processing");
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn) // returns undefined
function ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn) {
        var shipFrom = isReturn ? 'Return To' : 'Ship From';
        var shipTo = isReturn ? 'Pickup From' : 'Ship To';
        $('ul.nav.nav-tabs').find('li[heading="Ship From"]:visible > a').first().text(shipFrom);
        $('ul.nav.nav-tabs').find('li[heading="Ship To"]:visible > a').first().text(shipTo);
    }

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns undefined
function ClientBusinessRules() {

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
    }

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        var shipment = new Shipment(shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipment.UserRef1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = shipment.UserRef2;
    }

    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
    }

    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
    }



    class Shipment {
        constructor(shipmentRequest) {
            this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
        }
        
        get UserEmail() { return this.GetEmail(); }
        
        get Attn() { return this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Contact; }
        
        get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
        get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
        get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
        get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
        get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
        get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
        get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
        get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
        get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
        get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

        get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
        get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
        get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
        get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
        get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
        get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
        get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
        get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
        get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
        get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

        get PkgRef1() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference; }
        get PkgRef2() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference; }

        get PkgMisc1() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1; }
        get PkgMisc2() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2; }
        get PkgMisc3() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3; }
        get PkgMisc4() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4; }
        get PkgMisc5() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5; }
        get PkgMisc6() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6; }
        get PkgMisc7() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7; }
        get PkgMisc8() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8; }
        get PkgMisc9() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9; }
        get PkgMisc10() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10; }

        get PkgMisc11() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11; }
        get PkgMisc12() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12; }
        get PkgMisc13() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference13; }
        get PkgMisc14() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14; }
        get PkgMisc15() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference15; }
        get PkgMisc16() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16; }
        get PkgMisc17() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; }
        get PkgMisc18() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; }
        get PkgMisc19() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; }
        get PkgMisc20() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; }

        GetEmail() {
            var emailText = "";
            var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            Array.from(tags).forEach(function (tag) {
                if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
            });
            return emailText;
        }



        GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
            var returnValue = "";
            var customData = null;
            if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
            if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

            if (customData) {
                customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                    if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
                })
            }
            return returnValue;
        }
        // End Shipment Class
    }

    class ViewModel {
        constructor(viewModel) {
            this.VM = viewModel;
        }

        IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
            var isValid = false;
            if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
                var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations
                options.forEach(function (option) {
                    if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
                });
            }

            if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
            return isValid;
        }

        // End ViewModel Class
    }

    // End ClientBusinessRules
}

        this.vm.hideSaveAddress = true;
        this.vm.isUpdateAddressBookEntry = true;
        this.vm.hideAddressSearch = true;
        this.vm.thirdPartyBillingDisabled = thirdPartyBillingDisabled;
        debugger;

        client.shipping.consignee.validateAddress.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.ValidateAddress);

        function thirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) {
            var $tpb = $('div[property="ThirdPartyBilling"]');
            if (isDisabled) {
                this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
                this.thirdPartyBilling();
                $tpb.find('input').attr('disabled', true);
                $tpb.find('label').addClass('disabled');
            } else {
                $tpb.find('input').removeAttr('disabled');
                $tpb.find('label').removeClass('disabled');
            }
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {
    this.vm.shipMode = 0;
    this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
    filterPickupPaymentType();

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            var list = ['Pay by shipper account'];            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var currencies = $('[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option');
                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }
}

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns undefined
//Select Service in Service List Box 
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns undefined
//Set Currency to CAD
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// loadValueFocus() // returns void
            loadValueFocus: function () { client.focus(this.loadValue) },

// consigneeCompanyFocus() // returns void
            consigneeCompanyFocus: function () { client.focus(this.consigneeCompany) }

// focus(selector) // returns void
        focus: function (selector) {
            if (setFocus(selector) == 0) {
                var intervalId = setInterval(function () {
                    if (setFocus(selector)) clearInterval(intervalId)
                }, 10)
            }

            function setFocus(selector) {
                var element = $(selector);
                element.focus();
                return element.length;
            }
        }

// InitializeDelegateFunctions() // returns void
  InitializeDelegateFunctions = () =>
  {
    let that = this;
    this.DataStore = new DataStore(this.H);
    this.Dialogs = new UserDialogs(this);

    this.LoadSampleData();

    //create the first container object
    this.Containers.Create(1);

    //if the elements exist at the time of rendering, use .on
    $('#btnAddMultipleItems').on('click', function(e) { that.Dialogs.Show('MultipleOperationsDialog'); });
    $('#btnRemoveMultipleItems').on('click', function(e) { that.Dialogs.Show('MultipleOperationsDialog', true); });
    $('#btnDev').on('click', function(e)
    {
      let post = new PostBack();
      const p = post.SessionData(that.Containers.List).then((ret) => console.log(ret));
      //that.Dialogs.Dialog.Show('PackingCompleteDialog');
    });

    //change the ShipExec logo to remove the overlay and show the standard shipping screen
    $('div.navbar-header').find('a[href="/ShipExecThinClient/"]').attr('href', '').on('click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();
      that.ShowStandardShippingScreen();
    });

    //*** DEVELOPMENT CODE ONLY.  REMOVE BEFORE PROD */
    $('body').delegate('td.item-number', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let tr = $(this).closest('tr').data();
      that.Items.Add(tr);
    });

    $('body').on('click', function(e)
    {
      let target = e.target;

      let bDropdown = $(target).closest('div').hasClass('dropdown');

      bDropdown = bDropdown || $(target).closest('span').hasClass('dropdown');

      if (bDropdown) { return false; }

      $('.dropdown-menu').slideUp();

      if ($('#inputFilterTerm').is(':focus'))
      {
        return false;
      }
      else
      {
        $('.escape-target').hide();
      }
    });

    /**
     * Button click events.
     */
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('.btn-cancel', 'click', function(e)
    {
      $(this).closest('.dialog').fadeOut().find('input').val([]);
      $(that.Overlay.Hide());
    });

    //this handles the dynamic updates on the list items to show a tooltip wtih item information
    $(this.H.UIContainer).on('shown.bs.tooltip', function(e)
    {
      if ($(e.target).hasClass('li-item-number'))
      {
        const c = +$(e.target).siblings('.li-item-count').first().text().replace(/[^0-9.]+/g, '');
        $('div.tooltip').find('.item-count').text(c || 1);
      }
    })

    $('#spanFilterItems').on('click', function(e)
    {
      that.RowFilterModal.Show();
    });

    $('.dropdown').on('click', function(e)
    {
      $(this).find('.dropdown-menu').first().slideToggle();
    })

    $('#ulTableColumnDropdownMenu > li > a').on('click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      $(this).find('i').toggleClass('inactive');

      that.ToggleColumnVisibility($(this).attr('sos-key'));
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=AddContainerToShipment]', 'click', function()
    {
      that.Containers.Create();
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=RemoveItemFromContainer]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const data = $(this).closest('li').data();
      const parent = +$(this).closest('div.container-parent').attr('container-index');

      let json = {
        DialogType: $(this).attr('event'),
        Data: data,
        ContainerIndex: parent
      };

      that.Dialogs.Show('ConfirmationDialog', json);
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=RemoveContainerFromShipment]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let container = $(this).closest('.container-parent').attr('container-index');

      let json = {};
      json.DialogType = $(this).attr('event');
      json.ContainerIndex = container;

      that.Dialogs.Show('ConfirmationDialog', json);
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=SetActiveContainer]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const parent = $(this).closest('div.container-parent').attr('container-index');

      if ($(e.target).hasClass('glyphicon') || $(e.target).closest('div.container-parent').hasClass('active'))
      {
        e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); e.stopImmediatePropagation();
        return false;
      }

      that.SetActiveContainer(parent);
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=CloseContainer]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const parent = $(this).closest('div.container-parent').first().attr('container-index');
      that.Dialogs.Show('CloseContainerDialog', parent);
    });

    //event handler for moving the toast notification around
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('.draggable', 'mousedown', function(e)
    {
      var dr = $(this).addClass("drag");

      let height = dr.outerHeight();
      let width = dr.outerWidth();

      let ypos = dr.offset().top + height - e.pageY;
      let xpos = dr.offset().left + width - e.pageX;

      $(document.body).on('mousemove', function(e)
      {
        var itop = e.pageY + ypos - height;
        var ileft = e.pageX + xpos - width;

        if (dr.hasClass("drag"))
        {
          dr.offset({ top: itop, left: ileft });
        }
      }).on('mouseup', function(e)
      {
        dr.removeClass("drag");
      });
    });

    //when the user hovers over a row, highlight the matching row in the panel list items
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate(this.H.TableRowsAll, 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      const row = $(this).data();
      const containers = that.DataStore.GetContainersForFocusedItem(row.RowId);
      if (containers)
      {
        containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"]`).addClass('highlight'));
      }

      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          $(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveList).find(`.list-group-item[row-id="${row.RowId}"]`).addClass('item-hover');
          if (containers) containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"] .panel-body`).addClass('highlight'));
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          $(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveList).find(`.list-group-item[row-id="${row.RowId}"]`).removeClass('item-hover');
          if (containers) containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"] .panel-body`).removeClass('highlight'));
          break;
      }
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event="SetActiveContainer"]', 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          let i = $(this).closest('div.container-parent').attr('container-index');
          that.HighlightRowsInContainer(i);
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          that.HighlightRowsInContainer();
          break;
      }
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveListItems, 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          that.HighlightSelectedRow($(this).attr('row-id'));
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          that.HighlightSelectedRow();
          break;
      }
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ShowAllRows]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      $(that.H.TableId).find('tr.text-success').fadeToggle();
    });

    //this is here because of a bug in bootstrap where the dropdown will only work once
    //this replaces any native bootstrap button click event handler for dropdown-toggles
    $('button.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      $(this).siblings('ul:first').slideToggle(200)
    });

    /**
     * TODO:  Move this to the HTML class.
     */
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ShowContainerDetails]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const data = $(this).closest('.container-parent').data();
      const containerIndex = data[0].PackedItems[0].ContainerIndex;
      const productCount = Object.keys(data).length;

      let div = $('div.container-item-details').first();
      let itemCount = 0;

      //get rid of any existing entries
      $(div).find('.divTableRow').not('.template').remove();
      $(div).find('span.container-index').text(containerIndex);

      Object.keys(data).forEach((key) =>
      {
        let item = data[key];
        let count = item.PackedItems[0].Count;
        itemCount += count;
        let p = $(div).find('.divTableRow.template').first().clone();
        $(p).removeClass('template');

        $(p).find('span.item-count').text(count);
        $(p).find('span.item-number').text(item.ItemNumber);
        $(p).find('span.item-description').text(item.ItemDescription);

        $(p).appendTo(div)
      });

      $(div).find('.container-title').text(`${productCount} Product${productCount > 1 ? `s` : ``} | ${itemCount} Item${itemCount > 1 ? `s` : ``} | 36X48X72 | 1825 LBS`);

      that.Overlay.Show();

      $(div).fadeIn();
    });

    //*** END DEVELOPMENT CODE ONLY */

    //if the user comes back to the page, sometimes the dropdown will have duplicate values.  empty it here.
    $('#ulContainerList').find('ul:gt(0)').remove();

    $('#LocaleForm').find('.glyphicon').animate({ 'margin-left': '15px' }, 400);

    //this closes any elements with the class of .escape-target. used on popups, alerts, or divs
    $('body').delegate('#divPackVerifyOverlay', 'keydown keyup', function(e)
    {
      if (e.key == "Escape")
      {
        //clear out any filters
        if ($('#divFilterTableRowModal').is(':visible')) { $('#inputFilterTerm').val([]); /*that.FilterTableRowsByText();*/ }

        $('.escape-target').fadeOut();
      }
    });

    $('body').delegate('#inputBarcodeValue', 'keyup', function(e)
    {
      if ($(this).val().trim().length === 0) return false;

      let u = $(this).val().trim().toUpperCase();

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        that.AddItemToCurrentContainer(u);
      }
    });

    return;

    /* POST RE-WRITE EVENTS */



    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ShowOnlyThisContainer]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const rows = that.GetTableRowsInSelectedContainer(null, true);
      that.AppEvents.On_FilterTableRowsByContainer(rows, this.checked);
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=HideAlert]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      $(this).hide();
      $('div.overlay').hide();

      let tdtool = $(that.tableId).find('tr:eq(2)').find('td[data-toggle="tooltip"]:eq(0)');
      $(tdtool).tooltip('show');
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('#inputFilterTerm', 'keyup', function(e)
    {
      //show or hide the 'clear' anchor visibility
      $('[event="ClearTableFilters"]').toggle($(this).val().length > 0);

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        //the table rows filter as the user types so just need to hide the div when they press enter
        //the escape key is handled in another delegate as it applies to multiple elements
        $('#divFilterInput').hide();
      }

      const rows = that.GetTableRowsWithMatchingText($(this).val().toUpperCase());
      that.AppEvents.On_FilterTableRowsByText(rows);
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ClearTableFilters]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      $('#inputFilterTerm').val([]);
      $(that.Elements.TableRowsWithId).fadeIn('fast');
      $(this).hide();
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ShowItemPackingDetails]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let rowid = $(this).closest('tr').attr('row-id');
      that.ShowItemPackingDetails();
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=CollapsePanel]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      //rotate the icon 180 degrees
      $(this).toggleClass('up');

      let pb = $(this).closest('div.panel').find('div.panel-body');
      let ul = $(this).closest('div.panel').find('ul.list-group');

      //the visible element will be f...slide that one up, then slide down the other
      let f = null, n = null;
      if ($(pb).is(':visible')) { f = pb; n = ul; } else { f = ul; n = pb }

      $(f).slideToggle().promise().done(function(e)
      {
        $(n).slideToggle();
      });
    });

    //there are two ways to change the active container, either by selecting the option from the
    //table dropdown menu, or by clicking on the panel body in the open containers panel
    //because of this, handle them both here by adding .panel-body to the event handler
    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('ul.dropdown-menu > li > a', 'click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();

      let event = $(this).attr('event');
      let ci = +$(this).attr('container-index');

      //if there is no event associated with the anchor element
      //then the dropdown to select a table column was clicked
      //don't close the dropdown, but run the function to show the selected column

      /*
       $('td[sos-key="CSdescript"] div').animate({
            opacity: 0,
            left: "+=500",
            width: "toggle"
          }, 500, function() {
            // Animation complete.
          });
      */
      if (!event)
      {
        $(this).find('i').toggleClass('inactive');
        that.ToggleColumnVisibility($(this).attr('sos-key'));
        return;
      }

      $('ul.dropdown-menu').fadeOut();

    });

    //the temp dropdown for demo purposes.  remove before prod.
    $('[event="SelectOrderFromJson"]').closest('span').tooltip('show');
  }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) 
    {        
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            var aTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            var searchText = "Email";
            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
                    if (aTags[i].textContent == searchText) {
                        var loaded = aTags[i];
                        aTags[i].click();
                    }
                }
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
                }
            }, 50); 
        }
        
           if (location === '/batchmanager') {
            $( "#btnCreateNewBatches" ).click(function() {                
                var userMethodParams = { "action": "CreateNewBatchForProcessing"};
            
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
                var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    alert("Batch creation request sent");
                }
            });
            
            $("#btnSetBatchAsPrinted").click(function() {

            var batchId = $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text();
            
            if(batchId !== null && batchId !== '')
            {
                var proceedToSetBatchPrinted = confirm("Confirm to set batch" + batchId + " as deleted? Click OK to continue or Cancel");
                
                if(proceedToSetBatchPrinted)
                {
                    var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetBatchAsPrinted", "batchid" : $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text()};
        
                    var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
        
                    var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
        
                    if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
                    {
                        client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
                    } 
                    else 
                    {
                        alert(batchId + " was set to deleted");
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert("No batch has been selected");
            }
            }); // end function
        }
    }

           {
 $(document).delegate('li.uib-tab.nav-item[heading="Hazmat"] > a', 'click', function (e)
               {
                   debugger;
                       try
                       {
                            var key = vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.find(k=> k.Key == 'HAZ_CERT').Key;
                            var value = vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.find(k=> k.Key == 'HAZ_CERT').Value;
                            if(key == null || value != 'Y')
                            {
                                alert('Hazardous Shipping Requires User Certification Setup[HAZ_CERT]');

                        }
                   catch(err)

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
          var employeeID;
          var BU;
          var OU;
          var CR;
          var locationCode;
         var CustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
            for (var Custom in CustomData) {
                     if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom1") employeeID = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                      if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom2") BU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
             
         if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
            alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

        if ($welcome.length) {
            clearInterval(pageInterval);

        }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
 
        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                    vm.checkShip();                    
                }
            }
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();        
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();        
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void

    //if(location === "/")
     //document.location = "#!/shipping";

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        if (!angular.element('input[value="Get Weight"]').prop('disabled')){
            if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount == undefined) {
                vm.getWeight();
            }
        }
        var startTime = new Date();
        var weightExists = setInterval(() => {
            if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                clearInterval(weightExists);
            } else {
                if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount != undefined) {
                    startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);
                    vm.checkShip();
                    //$('#myShipBtn').click()
                }
            }
        }, 333);
    }

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		$("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked", false);
		$("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val("");

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

		$("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked", vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.UserData1 == "true");       
    }

// Source: Target (TARGET)_Target CBR_2489.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        
        const vm = this.vm;
        
        if (location == '/shipping') {

            shipping();
        }
        
        function shipping() {
            vm.AddReturnLabel = function () {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.push(getPackageObject());
            vm.totalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length;
            };

            vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function () {
                debugger;
                vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND" };
                if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                    vm.selectedServices = [];
                }
                vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };
            

            function getPackageObject() {
                debugger;
                let addedPackage = structuredClone(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0]);
                addedPackage.ReturnDelivery = true;
                addedPackage.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                return addedPackage;
            };

        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model*="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.style.border = null;
                });
            }
    }

// function getUserContext() // returns void
    function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

            // Domestic Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]', 'change', function () {

                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                } else {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                }
            });
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {

                $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });
            // International Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]', 'change', function () {
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]');
                //   alert($billOption.val());
                if ($billOption.val() == "thirdParty") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').show();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                } else {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                }
            });
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {

                $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });

            var startTime = new Date();
            var pageLoaded = setInterval(function () {
                if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                    clearInterval(pageLoaded);
                    //    console.log('clearinterval');
                } else {
                    var tpbFound = false;
                    var consigneeFound = false;
                    var $thirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');
                    var $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="DutiesAndTaxesThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');
                    var tpbSearchAddress = $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    var $consignee = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                    var consineeSearchAddress = $consignee.find('[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.length && tpbSearchAddress.length) {
                        tpbFound = true;
                    }

                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;


                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0) {
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                            //International
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() === '' || stateProvince.val() === '') && postalCode !== '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;

        dismissAlertDialog();

        if (location === '/shipping') {
            //consigneeStateIsRequired = vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired;


            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                $terms = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]')
                $termsOfSale = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].TermsOfSale"]');

                var $consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]')
                consigneeState = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                consigneeCountry = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="Country"]');
                miscReference8 = $('[property="MiscReference8"] input');
                returnLabel = $('label:contains("Return Label")');
                returnOption = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]');

                var loaded = $terms.length && $termsOfSale.length && consigneeState.length &&
                consigneeCountry.length && miscReference8.length && returnLabel.length && returnOption.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 50);
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        GetUserContext();
        if(location==="/shipping"){
            
            var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
            var chkShipNotification = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail"]');
            if (chkShipNotification)
            {
                /* Stop the timer. */
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                //debugger;
        $('body').delegate('[property="ShipNotificationEmail"]', 'click', function () {
             if($('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail"]').prop("checked")){
                $('[name="shipNotificationAddressEmail"]').val(getUserName()).change();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
             } else {
                 vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = "";
             }
        })

        $('body').delegate('[property="DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail"]', 'click', function () {
            if($('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail"]').prop("checked")){
                $('[name="DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail"]').val(getUserName()).change();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
            }else{
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = "";
            }

        })

        $('body').delegate('[property="DeliveryNotificationEmail"]', 'click', function () {
            if($('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail"]').prop("checked")){
                $('[name="DeliveryNotificationEmail"]').val(getUserName()).change();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();               
            }else{
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = "";     
            }

        })
            }
             
         }, 50); 
        }
        if(location==="/history"){
                     var reports = $('select[id="reports"]:eq(0)');
        var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
            
            if (reports)
            {
                /* Stop the timer. */
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('select[id="reports"]:eq(0) option:eq(0)').text("My History");
            }
             
         }, 50); 
        }
    }

// PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns void
    this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
        var selectedValue = $('select[id="reports"]:eq(0)').val();
        var selectedReport = $("select[id='reports'] option[value='" + selectedValue + "'");
        //debugger;
        if(selectedReport[0].innerText !=="All History"){
            searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 0 });
        }
    };

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {
    angular.element('a:contains("End of Day")').hide();
    //angular.element('a:contains("History")').hide();

    if (location === '/')
    {
      document.location = '#!/shipping';

// PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		//debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    //debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void

            this.Shipping();

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.profile.Services.sort(byService);

        $(client.shipping.buildShipmentModal).on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
            client.shipping.buildTotalPackagesFocus();
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function byService(a, b) {
            var sortingArr = [
                "UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Three-Day Select (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Ground (UPS Adapter)"
            ]
            return sortingArr.indexOf(a.Name) - sortingArr.indexOf(b.Name);
        }

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() == '' || stateProvince.val() == '') && postalCode != '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {
            event.preventDefault();

            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // all shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }
    }
